| 0:01:49| Another big component of it is permit fees.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=109)|
| 0:01:53| The Clean Air Act 1990 amendments stated that industry facilities that were polluting the air would pay for that pollution.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=113)|
| 0:02:04| They assessed a certain dollar amount per ton of air pollutants that they put into the air.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=124)|
| 0:02:11| So that's where a large part of our fee budgets or our income is coming from.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=131)|
| 0:02:20| With industry shutting down throughout Knox County and actually all over, that has hurt us.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=140)|
| 0:02:29| Every time we lose an industry, we're losing their permit fees, too.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=149)|
| 0:02:33| So we don't like to see that either.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090512budgethearings?start=153)|
